## 🔧 Most Common Issues (ALFA)

| [SIA-R56](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56): Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable | **99** of 100 | [View Rule](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56) |

## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 99 page(s) - 99 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate
**Issue**: All page content should be contained by landmarks

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<section class="padding-none">
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
.padding-none:nth-child(3)
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('.padding-none:nth-child(3)')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://gnb.ca/en/campaign/accessibility.html
- https://gnb.ca/en/campaign/geonb/support-services.html
- https://gnb.ca/en/campaign/accessibility/accessibility-advisory-board.html
- https://gnb.ca/en/campaign/accessibility/accessibility-resources.html
- https://gnb.ca/en/campaign/accessibility/disability-numbers.html
- *...and 94 more page(s)*

---

#### Pattern 2: Affects 98 page(s) - 98 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a class="cmp-list__item-link" data-cmp-clickable="" href="/en/admin/disclaimer.html">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a[@class="cmp-list__item-link"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a[@class="cmp-list__item-link"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

#### Pattern 5: Affects 98 page(s) - 98 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate
**Issue**: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<nav class="skip-link">
        <a href="#main" class="gnb-btn">Skip to main content</a>
    </nav>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
.skip-link
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools

#### Pattern 8: Affects 98 page(s) - 98 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [skip-link](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/skip-link?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate
**Issue**: The skip-link target should exist and be focusable

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a href="#main" class="gnb-btn">Skip to main content</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
a[href$="#main"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('a[href$="#main"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://gnb.ca/en/campaign/accessibility.html

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://gnb.ca/

#### Rule: [SIA-R59](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r59)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not have a heading element

### https://gnb.ca/en/campaign/accessibility.html

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="cmp-list__item-link" href="/en/campaign/accessibility.html#1">Overview</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="cmp-list__item-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/en/gov/engagement-consultation/consultation-accessibility.html">View open opportunities</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R113](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r113)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size and spacing
- HTML: `<a class="cmp-list__item-link" data-cmp-clickable="" href="/en/admin/privacy.html">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="cmp-list__item-link"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R53: Headings follow a logical hierarchy](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53)
**WCAG**: Best Practice

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h4>Engagement opportunities</h4>`
- XPath: `/h4`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R61](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.4.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/bypass-blocks) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<iframe title="reCAPTCHA" width="304" height="78" role="presentation" name="a-1t5wzgon52le" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" sandbox="allow-forms allow-popups allow-same-origin allow-scripts allow-top-navigation allow-modals allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox allow-storage-access-by-user-activation" src="https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api2/anchor?ar=1&k=6LcVeXkjAAAAABLbh6-N6eormRz0yrVHf6XWCHb9&co=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuZ25iLmNhOjQ0Mw..&hl=en&v=QvLuXwupqtKCyjBw2xIzFLIf&size=normal&anchor-ms=20000&execute-ms=30000&cb=jywvzxcbd6ft" />`

**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="cmp-breadcrumb__item-link" itemprop="item" data-cmp-clickable="" href="/en.html">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="cmp-breadcrumb__item-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="cmp-list__item-link" href="/en/topic/education-training/jobs-in-education/internationally-educated.html#1">Overview</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="cmp-list__item-link"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R113](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r113)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size and spacing
- HTML: `<a class="cmp-list__item-link" data-cmp-clickable="" href="/en/admin/privacy.html">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="cmp-list__item-link"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R61](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R61](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

### https://gnb.ca/en/topic/health-wellness/sexual-health/abortion.html

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="cmp-breadcrumb__item-link" itemprop="item" data-cmp-clickable="" href="/en.html">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="cmp-breadcrumb__item-link"]`

- XPath: `/a[@class="external-link"]`

- Message: Target has insufficient size and spacing

- XPath: `/a[@class="cmp-list__item-link"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://gnb.ca/

#### Rule: [page-has-heading-one](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/page-has-heading-one?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Page should contain a level-one heading
- HTML: `<html class="no-js" dir="ltr" lang="en-US" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">`
- XPath: `html`

### https://gnb.ca/en/campaign/accessibility.html

#### Rule: [heading-order](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/heading-order?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h4>Engagement opportunities</h4>`
- XPath: `h4`

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<nav class="skip-link">         <a href="#main" class="gnb-btn">Skip to main content</a>     </nav>`
- XPath: `.skip-link`

#### Rule: [list](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/list?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/info-and-relationships) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: <ul> and <ol> must only directly contain <li>, <script> or <template> elements
- HTML: `<ul id="gnbList-12e576356b" data-cmp-data-layer="{"list-12e576356b":{"@type":"core/wcm/components/list/v4/list","repo:modifyDate":"2025-12-03T17:28:57Z"}}" class="gnb-page-nav cmp-list list-12e576356b">`
- XPath: `#gnbList-12e576356b`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<section class="padding-none">`
- XPath: `.padding-none:nth-child(3)`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<label class="visually-hidden" for="q">New Brunswick Site Search</label>`
- XPath: `label`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<input type="text" onclick="this.value='';" name="q" placeholder="Search" class="searchText ui-autocomplete-input" id="q" autocomplete="off">`
- XPath: `#q`

#### Rule: [skip-link](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/skip-link?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The skip-link target should exist and be focusable
- HTML: `<a href="#main" class="gnb-btn">Skip to main content</a>`
- XPath: `a[href$="#main"]`

- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<section class="padding-none">`
- XPath: `.padding-none:nth-child(3)`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<label class="visually-hidden" for="q">New Brunswick Site Search</label>`
- XPath: `label`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<input type="text" onclick="this.value='';" name="q" placeholder="Search" class="searchText ui-autocomplete-input" id="q" autocomplete="off">`
- XPath: `#q`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="">`
- XPath: `#container-fb4d07a95e > div:nth-child(6)`

- HTML: `<label class="visually-hidden" for="q">New Brunswick Site Search</label>`
- XPath: `label`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<input type="text" onclick="this.value='';" name="q" placeholder="Search" class="searchText ui-autocomplete-input" id="q" autocomplete="off">`
- XPath: `#q`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="">`
- XPath: `div:nth-child(6)`

#### Rule: [skip-link](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/skip-link?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The skip-link target should exist and be focusable
- HTML: `<a href="#main" class="gnb-btn">Skip to main content</a>`
- XPath: `.gnb-btn`

### https://gnb.ca/en/topic/health-wellness/sexual-health/abortion.html

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<nav class="skip-link">         <a href="#main" class="gnb-btn">Skip to main content</a>     </nav>`
- XPath: `.skip-link`

#### Rule: [list](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/list?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/info-and-relationships) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: <ul> and <ol> must only directly contain <li>, <script> or <template> elements
- HTML: `<ul id="gnbList-f0b357ea0e" data-cmp-data-layer="{"list-f0b357ea0e":{"@type":"core/wcm/components/list/v4/list","repo:modifyDate":"2025-12-18T18:23:52Z"}}" class="gnb-page-nav cmp-list list-f0b357ea0e">`
- XPath: `#gnbList-f0b357ea0e`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<section class="padding-none">`
- XPath: `.padding-none:nth-child(3)`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<label class="visually-hidden" for="q">New Brunswick Site Search</label>`

- XPath: `.gnb-btn`
